to make a trade in the NFL Draft\n\t\t<span style=\"font-weight:normal\">\n\t\t\tPosted By: <a href=\"/forums/member.php?action=mailform&amp;userid=8\" title=\"\" target=\"_blank\">Dan in Lafayette</a>\n\t\t\tPosted On Today</span>\n\t\t<span class=\"time\">12:41 AM</span>\n\t</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n\t<td class=\"alt1\" width=\"100%\">\n\t\t<table cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" border=\"0\" width=\"100%\">\n\t\t<tbody><tr>\n\t\t\t<td class=\"alt1\" valign=\"top\" align=\"justify\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div align=\"left\"><img src=\"http://saintsreport.com/images/topics/draft.gif\" border=\"0\" alt=\"\"><br>\n<br>\n<b>By Dan Benton -- Larry Brown Sports</b><br>\n<br>\nThe NFL Draft is always full of surprises. From the picks themselves to the wildly unexpected trade deals, it’s nearly impossible to predict what will unfold in the draft. Of course, that’s what makes it so much fun for fans and analysts alike.<br>\n<br>\nEvery year, there seem to be a handful of trades no one saw coming. Teams either look to move up to acquire a specific talent or they look to trade down in hopes of landing additional picks.<br>\n<br>\nThe 2017 NFL Draft is not going to be any different in that regard, so the expectation should be that several deals will be made. But who is the most likely to be involved in such deals? line of scrimmage, the godfathers of today's box safeties were men like John Lynch, LeRoy Butler, Steve Atwater and Darren Woodson.<br>\n<br>\nBut the roles are expanding now. A safety in today's game might be deployed at strongside linebacker, as a nickel back covering slot receivers, a center fielder playing deep or a blitzer off the edge. New Orleans Saints strong safety Kenny Vaccaro played just about all of those roles last season, along with a few more.<br>\n<br>\nNFL teams are looking for more players like him.<br>\n<br>\n<a expecting to hear his name called during the 2017 NFL draft, which will last from next Thursday to April 29.<br>\n<br>\nThe draft will begin with Round 1 on Thursday.<br>\n<br>\nRounds 2 and 3 will be April 28 and Rounds 4-7 will be April 29. It will be televised on ESPN and the NFL Network.<br>\n<br>\nMcGuire, who enjoyed record-setting careers during his time as a player at Vandebilt Catholic High School and the University of Louisiana at Lafayette, knows his name could be called in any of the NFL’s seven draft rounds.<br>\n<br>\nWhen it does, McGuire, who played running back in college and is projected as one in the NFL, said it will be a moment that will change his life forever.<br>\n<br>\n<a href=\"http://www.houmatoday.com/news/20170420/houma-native-expected-to-be-drafted-into-nfl\" target=\"_blank\"><b>Full Article -- But, the front office has to consider a future without Brees knowing how few quarterbacks succeed into their 40s.<br>\n<br>\nTeams take different approaches to securing their long-term plans at quarterback, and Phil Savage, the former Cleveland Browns general manager, said the Saints have to consider what their timeline looks like as they decide whether to draft*a signal caller in 2017.<br>\n<br>\n<a href=\"http://www.nola.com/saints/index.ssf/2017/04/should_saints_draft_drew_brees.html#incart_river_index\" target=\"_blank\"><b>Full Article -- valign=\"top\" align=\"justify\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div align=\"left\"><img src=\"http://saintsreport.com/images/topics/nf_im.jpg\" border=\"0\" alt=\"\"><br>\n<br>\n<b>By Jeff Howe -- Boston Globe</b><br>\n<br>\nFOXBORO — The Patriots aren’t willing to openly disclose their plans for cornerback Malcolm Butler and quarterback Jimmy Garoppolo.<br>\n<br>\nWithout a pick in the first two rounds of next week’s draft, the Patriots are equipped with a pair of significant trade chips that could net them some quality ammunition in the early rounds. <br>\n<br>\nAnd with a development in Butler’s situation yesterday, the Patriots can begin fielding trade offers.<br>\n<br>\nButler signed his restricted free agent tender, which served as the next logical step in the layered process of finding his home for the 2017 season. Rather than waiting until Friday’s deadline in the hope of landing an offer sheet, Butler inked the tender to give the Patriots an extra few days to negotiate any trade calls prior to the draft. The Saints have been openly interested in acquiring Butler, who visited their facility in New Orleans for two days last month.<br>\n<br>\n<a href=\"http://www.bostonherald.com/sports/patriots/2017/04/patriots_noncommittal_on_malcolm_butler_as_cb_signs_tenders\" target=\"_blank\"><b>Full Article -- Globe</b></a></div>\n\t\t\t</td>\n\t\t</tr>\n\t\t</tbody></table>\n\t\t<div class=\"smallfont\" style=\"font-weight:bold;text-align:right\">\n\t\t\t<a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://saintsreport.com/forums/f11/patriots-noncommittal-malcolm-butler-cb-signs-tenders-367244-print/?threadid=367244\" title=\"Printable Version\"><img class=\"inlineimg\" src=\"http://srgrey.saintsreportcom.netdna-cdn.com/buttons/printer.gif\" alt=\"Printable Version\" border=\"0\" title=\"Printable Version\"></a>\n\t\t\t<a href=\"/forums/sendmessage.php?do=sendtofriend&amp;t=367244\" rel=\"nofollow\" title=\"Email A Friend\"><img class=\"inlineimg\" src=\"http://srgrey.saintsreportcom.netdna-cdn.com/buttons/sendtofriend.gif\" alt=\"Email This Article To Someone\" border=\"0\" title=\"Email This Article To Someone\"></a>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t<a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"/modules/News/showarticle.php?threadid=367244\" title=\"Read full article\">Read More...</a>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n\t<td class=\"thead\" style=\"padding:1px\"><img src=\"/images/clear_dot.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"1\" height=\"1\"></td>\n</tr>\n\n</tbody></table>\n\t\t\n\t\t\n\t\t\t<table class=\"tborder\" cellpadding=\"6\" cellspacing=\"1\" border=\"0\" width=\"100%\" style=\"border-top:0px\">\n\t\t\t<tbody><tr>\n\t\t\t\t<td class=\"tfoot\" align=\"right\"><a href=\"/modules/News/index.php\" title=\"Read All News\">More...</a></td>\n\t\t\t</tr>\n\t\t\t</tbody></table>\n\t\t\n\t</div>\n</div><div style=\"margin:0px; In the 2017 NFL draft class, what jumps out to me is the huge amount of potential pro prospects with Louisiana roots available to the 32 NFL teams.<br>\n\t<br>\nSix out of the last nine years Louisiana per capita has produced more NFL players than any other state in the United States. In those 3 other years they came in second.<br>\n\t<br>\nI have never seen so many potential Louisiana pro prospects in my 30 years covering the college football world in one draft class. Below are prospects who played high school football and grew up in Louisiana.\t<br>\n\t<br>\n<b>In my potential top-30 prospects Louisiana has 4:</b><br>\n\t<br>\nLeonard Fournette-Halfback,\t\tLSU\t\t(St. Augustine)<br>\nTim Williams- Outside Linebacker,\tAlabama\t(University Lab)<br>\nCam Robinson-Offensive Tackle,\t\tAlabama\t(West Monroe)<br>\nTre’Davious White-Cornerback,\t\tLSU\t\t(Green Oaks-Shreveport)<br>\n\t<br>\n <br>\n<b>Prospects considered to be selected in the second or third round of the 2017 NFL draft Louisiana has 6 in:</b><br>\n <br>\nMalachi Dupre-Wide Receiver,\t\tLSU\t\t(John Curtis)<br>\nDavon Godchaux-Defensive Tackle,\tLSU\t\t(Plaquemine)<br>\nJeremy Cutrer-Cornerback,\t       Middle Tennessee\t(Jewel-Sumner-Kentwood)<br>\nDuke Riley-Outside Linebacker,\t\tLSU\t\t(John Curtis)<br>\nCarlos Henderson-Wide Receiver,     Louisiana Tech\t(McDonogh 35)<br>\nKendell Beckwith-Middle Linebacker,  \tLSU\t\t(East Feliciana)<br>\n<br>\n <br>\n<b>NFL prospects with very late third round into the fifth round Louisiana has 6 prospects:</b><br>\n <br>\nTanzel Smart-Defensive Tackle,\t\tTulane\t\t(Scotlandville Magnet)<br>\nChad Williams-Wide Receiver,\t\tGrambling\t(Madison Prep)<br>\nElijah McGuire-Halfback,\t\t\tUL-Lafayette\t(Vandebilt-Catholic)<br>\nTrent Taylor-Wide Receiver,\t\tLouisiana Tech\t(Evangel Christian)<br>\nTravin Dural-Wide Receiver,\t\tLSU\t\t(Breaux Bridge)<br>\nXavier Woods-Strong Safety,\t\tLouisiana Tech\t(West Monroe)<br>\n<br>\n <br>\n<b>Prospects with either sixth or seventh round pick grades Louisiana has 7 potential draft choices:</b><br>\n <br>\nCameron Tom-Offensive Center,\t    Southern Mississippi\t(Catholic High B.R.)<br>\nD’Nerius Antoine-Strong Safety,\t    Southern Mississippi\t(Westgate)<br>\nCethan Carter-Tight End,\t\t\tNebraska\t(Rummel)<br>\nJosh Boutte-Offensive Guard,\t\tLSU\t\t(Westgate)<br>\nB.J. Singleton-Defensive Tackle,\t\tHouston\t(Destrehan)<br>\nLenard Tillery-Halfback,\t\t\tSouthern\t(McKinley)<br>\nDwayne Thomas-Cornerback,\t\tLSU\t\t(O. Perry Walker) <br>\n <br>\n <br>\n<b>Prospects who just missed out on late round pick grades and will be signed as NFL free agents Louisiana has 5 in:</b><br>\n <br>\nSpeedy Noil-Wide Receiver/Return Man,\t\tTexas A&amp;M\t(Edna Karr)<br>\nDeSean Smith-Tight End,\t\t\t\tLSU\t\t(Barbe)<br>\nRickey Jefferson-Free Safety,\t\t\tLSU\t\t(Destrehan)<br>\nLazedrick Thompson-Halfback,\t\t\tTulane\t\t(St. Charles Catholic)<br>\nOtha Peters-Outside/Inside Linebacke,r\t                    UL-Lafayette\t(Covington)<br>\n <br>\nThe above numbers are just remarkable for our state to produce in one draft class.<br>\n<br>\n<br>\n<b>Watch for Engram</b><br>\n<br>\nI know the New Orleans Saints need help on the defensive side of the ball, but we all know Sean Payton loves offensive players and this is an offense-driven league. In Round 2 of the 2017 NFL draft don’t be surprised to see the Saints take a long look at Ole Miss tight end Evan Engram, if he is still on the board. <br>\n<br>\nThe 6-3, 230 pound Engram has re-written the Rebel records for receptions for tight ends and he wowed the scouts in Mobile, Alabama this past week at...</font>\n\t\t\t<a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"/modules/News/showarticle.php?threadid=364384\" title=\"NFL Prospects from THE BOOT -- Mike Detillier\"><strong>Read More...</strong></a>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</td>\n\t\n\n\t\n\t<td class=\"alt2\" width=\"50%\" valign=\"top\">\n\t\t<div class=\"smallfont\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\"><img src=\"http://srgrey.saintsreportcom.netdna-cdn.com/editor/insertimage.gif\" border=\"0\" alt=\"\" class=\"attach\" align=\"left\" style=\"margin:0px;padding:0px;padding-right:2px\"></a><strong>Mike Detillier's Top 85 Players of the 2017 NFL Draft</strong><br>\n\t\t\tPosted On 01-28-2017<br>\n\t\t\t<img src=\"http://saintsreport.com/images/topics/askmike.jpg\" border=\"0\" alt=\"\"><br>\n<br>\n<font size=\"2\"><b>Top 85 Players of the 2017 NFL Draft<br>\n<br>\nBy Mike Detillier</b><br>\n<br>\n<br>\n1.
